0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIntroduce \"warning\" system for disruptive rules (read more below)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eChange rule to a \"warning\": Require let or const instead of var (\u003ca href=\"https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-var\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eno-var\u003c/a\u003e) \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/633\" data-hovercard-type=\"issue\" data-hovercard-url=\"/standard/standard/issues/633/hovercard\"\u003e#633\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e treats all rule violations as errors, which means that \u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e\nwill exit with a non-zero (error) exit code.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eHowever, we may occasionally release a new major version of \u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e\nwhich changes a rule that affects the majority of \u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e users (for example,\ntransitioning from \u003ccode\u003evar\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003elet\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003econst\u003c/code\u003e). We do this only when we think the\nadvantage is worth the cost and only when the rule is\n\u003ca href=\"https://standardjs.com/#is-there-an-automatic-formatter\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eauto-fixable\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIn these situations, we have a \"transition period\" where the rule change is only\na \"warning\". Warnings don't cause \u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e to return a non-zero (error)\nexit code. However, a warning message will still print to the console. During\nthe transition period, \u003ccode\u003eusing standard --fix\u003c/code\u003e will update your code so that it's\nready for the next major version.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe slow and careful approach is what we strive for with \u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e. We're\ngenerally extremely conservative in enforcing the usage of new language\nfeatures. We want using \u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e to be light and fun and so we're careful\nabout making changes that may get in your way. As always, you can\n\u003ca href=\"https://standardjs.com/#how-do-i-disable-a-rule\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003edisable a rule\u003c/a\u003e at any time, if necessary.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v15.0.1...v16.0.0\"\u003e16.0.0\u003c/a\u003e - 2020-10-28\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-1600---2020-10-28\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: 16.0.0 - 2020-10-28\" href=\"#1600---2020-10-28\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWe're super excited to announce \u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e 16!\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAs with every new major release, there are lots of new rules in 16.0.0 designed\nto help catch bugs and make programmer intent more explicit. As a result, the eslint team has decided to drop support for it.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTo prevent breaking CI for projects which still support Node 6, \u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e silently passes when run by an unsupported version of Node.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFor \u003ccode\u003eeslint-config-standard\u003c/code\u003e users only:\u003c/strong\u003e Plugins are no longer affected by \u003ccode\u003eeslint\u003c/code\u003e's location\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePreviously, ESLint loaded plugins relative to the location of the ESLint package itself. As a result, we suggested that users with global ESLint installations should also install plugins globally, and users with local ESLint installations should install plugins locally.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eWith ESLint v6, plugins should always be installed locally, even if ESLint was installed globally. More precisely, ESLint v6 resolves plugins relative to the end user’s project by default, and always resolves shareable configs and parsers relative to the location of the config file that imports them.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSee \u003ca href=\"https://eslint.org/docs/user-guide/migrating-to-6.0.0#-plugins-and-shareable-configs-are-no-longer-affected-by-eslints-location\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003emigrating to ESLint 6.0.0 for more information\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThe documentation is now available in Japanese 🇯🇵!\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThanks to \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/munierujp\"\u003e@munierujp\u003c/a\u003e for the excellent work!\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eOther community contributed translations exist in Spanish, French, Italian, Korean, Portuguese, Simplified Chinese, and Taiwanese 10.0.0!\u003c/strong\u003e 🎉\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAs with every new major release, there are lots of new rules in 10.0.0 designed to\nhelp catch bugs and make programmer intent more explicit.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e is more popular than ever – \u003cstrong\u003e330,000 downloads per month!\u003c/strong\u003e It's even\nmore popular – \u003cstrong\u003e670,000 downloads per month\u003c/strong\u003e – if you include the\n\u003ca href=\"https://www.npmjs.com/package/eslint-config-standard\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eshareable ESLint config\u003c/a\u003e\nthat we also publish.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe most important change in 10.0.0 is that \u003cstrong\u003eusing deprecated Node.js APIs is now\nconsidered an error\u003c/strong\u003e. It's finally time to update those dusty old APIs!\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eDeprecated APIs are problematic because they may print warning messages in the\nconsole in recent versions of Node.js. This often confuses users and leads to\nunnecessary support tickets for project maintainers.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSome deprecated APIs are even insecure (or at least prone to incorrect usage) which\ncan have serious security implications. For that reason, \u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e now considers\nusage of \u003ccode\u003eBuffer(num)\u003c/code\u003e to be an error, since this function returns uninitialized\nprogram memory which could contain confidential information like passwords or keys.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eInstead of \u003ccode\u003eBuffer(num)\u003c/code\u003e, consider using \u003ccode\u003eBuffer.alloc(num)\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003eBuffer.from(obj)\u003c/code\u003e\nwhich make the programmer's intent clearer. These functions exist in all currently\nsupported versions of Node.js, including Node.js 4.x. For more background,\n\u003ca href=\"https://github.com/nodejs/node/issues/4660\" data-hovercard-type=\"issue\" data-hovercard-url=\"/nodejs/node/issues/4660/hovercard\"\u003esee this Node.js issue\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWe also improved some rules to support common patterns in code bases that use\nReact, JSX, and Flow.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhen you upgrade, consider running \u003ccode\u003estandard --fix\u003c/code\u003e to automatically fix some of\nthe issues caught by this new version.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv If you ever used\n\u003ca href=\"https://www.npmjs.com/package/standard-format\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estandard-format\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\nand ran into issues with the lack of ES2015+ support, you'll be happy about\n\u003ccode\u003e--fix\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estandard --fix\u003c/code\u003e is built into \u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e v8.0.0 for maximum convenience, it\nsupports ES2015, and it's lightweight (no additional dependencies since it's part\nof ESLint which powers \u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e). Lots of problems are already fixable, and more\nare getting added with each ESLint release.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e also outputs a message (\"Run \u003ccode\u003estandard --fix\u003c/code\u003e to automatically fix\nsome problems.\") when it detects problems that can be fixed automatically so you\ncan save time!\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWith \u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e v8.0.0, we are also dropping support for Node.js versions prior to\nv4. Node.js 0.10 and 0.12 are in maintenance mode and will be unsupported at the\nend of 2016. Node.js 4 is the current LTS version. If you are using an older\nversion of Node.js, we recommend upgrading to at least Node.js 4 as soon as\npossible. If you are unable to upgrade to Node.js 4 or higher, then we recommend\ncontinuing to use \u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e v7.x until you are ready to upgrade Node.js.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eImportant:\u003c/strong\u003e We will not be updating the \u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e v7.x versions going forward.\nAll bug fixes and enhancements will land in \u003ccode\u003estandard\u003c/code\u003e v8.x.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFull changelog below. Changelog","","All notable changes to this project will be documented in this file.","","The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/),","and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).","","## [17.1.0] - 2023-05-29","","- Update [`eslint-config-standard`](https://github.com/standard/eslint-config-standard) from `17.0.0` to `17.1.0`","","## [17.0.0] - 2022-04-20","","We're super excited to announce `standard` 17!","","This major release fully focuses on getting in sync with the wider ESLint ecosystem","and doesn't in itself introduce any new rules or features.","","When you upgrade, consider running `standard --fix` to automatically format your","code to match the current set of rules.","","This is the first release by two of our `standard` co-maintainers @Divlo and @voxpelli. Buy them a cake if you run into them, thanks for getting this release out!","","### Major changes","","- `eslint-config-node` has been replaced with the up to date fork `eslint-config-n`. If you have used comments like `// eslint-disable-line node/no-deprecated-api` you now have to reference the `n/` rules instead.","- [`object-shorthand` rule](https://github.com/standard/eslint-config-standard/pull/166) (as warning)","- Use of ESLint 8, which allows for support for all of the latest syntax that ESLint 8 includes, such as top level `await` #1548 #1775","- `--verbose` by default","","### Changed features","","- Update `eslint` from `~7.18.0` to `^8.13.0`","- Update `eslint-config-standard` from `16.0.3` to `17.0.0` to adapt to ESLint 8","- Update `eslint-config-standard-jsx` from `10.0.0` to `^11.0.0` to adapt to ESLint 8","- Update `standard-engine` from `^14` to `^15.0.0` to adapt to ESLint 8, see [its `CHANGELOG`](https://github.com/standard/standard-engine/blob/master/CHANGELOG.md#1500-0-2021-11-30)","- Move from `eslint-plugin-node@~11.1.0` to `eslint-plugin-n@^15.1.0` to adapt to ESLint 8","- Update `eslint-plugin-import` from `~2.24.2` to `^2.26.0`","- Update `eslint-plugin-promise` from `~5.1.0` to `^6.0.0`","- Update `eslint-plugin-react` from `~7.25.1` to `^7.28.0`","","## [17.0.0-2] - 2022-02-03","","- Fix: Follow up to the fix of #1548 in `17.0.0-1` #1775","","## [17.0.0-1] - 2022-01-31","","- Fix: Ensure we support all of the latest syntax that ESLint 8 includes, such as top level `await` #1548","","## [17.0.0-0] - 2022-01-31","","We're finally able to offer a pre-release of ESLint 8 based `standard` 17!","","This major release fully focuses on getting in sync with the wider ESLint ecosystem","and doesn't in itself introduce any new rules or features.","","This pre-release exists to test out the ESLint 8 related changes and discover","possible backwards incompatible changes that comes with it and mitigate","unintended such before a stable release.","","When you upgrade, consider running `standard --fix` to automatically format your","code to match the current set of rules.","","### Changed features","","- Update `eslint` from `~7.18.0` to `^8.8.0`","- Update `eslint-config-standard` from `16.0.3` to `17.0.0-0` to adapt to ESLint 8","- Update `eslint-config-standard-jsx` from `10.0.0` to `11.0.0-0` to adapt to ESLint 8","- Update `standard-engine` from `^14` to `^15.0.0-0` to adapt to ESLint 8, see [its `CHANGELOG`](https://github.com/standard/standard-engine/blob/master/CHANGELOG.md#1500-0-2021-11-30)","","## [16.0.4] - 2021-10-03","","- Update `eslint` from `~7.13.1` to `~7.18.0`","- Update `eslint-config-standard` from `16.0.2` to `16.0.3`","- Update `eslint-plugin-import` from `~2.22.1` to `~2.24.2`","- Update `eslint-plugin-promise` from `~4.2.1` to `~5.1.0`","- Update `eslint-plugin-react` from `~7.21.5` to `~7.25.1`","","## [16.0.3] - 2020-11-17","","- Update `eslint` from `~7.12.1` to `~7.13.0`","- Relax rule: Enforce default parameters to be last [#1414](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1414)","","## [16.0.2] - 2020-11-11","","- Allow `standard` to run on Node 11, even though it's not officially supported [#1597](https://github.com/standard/standard/pull/1597)","","## [16.0.1] - 2020-10-30","","- Introduce \"warning\" system for disruptive rules (read more below)","- Change rule to a \"warning\": Require let or const instead of var ([no-var](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-var)) [#633](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/633)","","`standard` treats all rule violations as errors, which means that `standard`","will exit with a non-zero (error) exit code.","","However, we may occasionally release a new major version of `standard`","which changes a rule that affects the majority of `standard` users (for example,","transitioning from `var` to `let`/`const`). We do this only when we think the","advantage is worth the cost and only when the rule is","[auto-fixable](https://standardjs.com/#is-there-an-automatic-formatter).","","In these situations, we have a \"transition period\" where the rule change is only","a \"warning\". Warnings don't cause `standard` to return a non-zero (error)","exit code. However, a warning message will still print to the console. During","the transition period, `using standard --fix` will update your code so that it's","ready for the next major version.","","The slow and careful approach is what we strive for with `standard`. We're","generally extremely conservative in enforcing the usage of new language","features. We want using `standard` to be light and fun and so we're careful","about making changes that may get in your way. As always, you can","[disable a rule](https://standardjs.com/#how-do-i-disable-a-rule) at any time, if necessary.","","## [16.0.0] - 2020-10-28","","We're super excited to announce `standard` 16!","","As with every new major release, there are lots of new rules in 16.0.0 designed","to help catch bugs and make programmer intent more explicit. This release brings","better performance, tons of bug fixes, improved JSX, React ⚛️, and Next.js support!","","When you upgrade, consider running `standard --fix` to automatically format your","code to match the newly added rules.","","❤️ If you enjoy StandardJS and want to support future releases, please","[support Feross](https://github.com/users/feross/sponsorship)!","","### New features","","- 🏎 Better performance: the filesystem doesn't need to be traversed multiple times! [#1023](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1023)","  - Massive improvements (on the order of minutes!) for projects with huge folders which are are ignored with `.gitignore`","","- 🌟 Support the `.gitignore` ignore syntax from the command line [#1117](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1117)","  - In older versions, the command `standard src` would not lint the `src/` folder","  - Instead, a glob pattern like `standard src/**/*.js` was required","  - This is now fixed! You can run `standard src` to lint the `src/` folder!","","- 🌟 Support relative paths from the command line in more situations (e.g. `standard ../src/*.js`) [#1384](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1384)","","- 🌟 New `extensions` option for linting additional extensions besides `.js`, `.jsx`, `.mjs`, and `.cjs`","  - Can be configured with the `--ext` command line flag or in `package.json`:","  - Example:","","    ```bash","    standard --ext .ts","    ```","","    ```json","    {","      \"standard\": {","        \"extensions\": [\".ts\"]","      }","    }","    ```","","- 🌟 New cache directory location, respecting `XDG_CACHE_HOME` preference, with fallback to `~/.cache/standard` [standard-engine/#214](https://github.com/standard/standard-engine/pull/214)","","### Changed features","","- Update `eslint` from `~7.11.0` to `~7.12.1`","","- Update `standard-engine` from `^12` to `^14`","  - Fix inaccurate `--help` command which indicates that `bundle.js` is automatically ignored when it is not anymore [standard-engine/#224](https://github.com/standard/standard-engine/pull/224)","  - Remove `deglob` package and use built-in ESLint folder-traversal support","","- Paths with square brackets (e.g. `[` and `]`) are no longer skipped [#1333](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1333)","  - This pattern is particularly common in Next.js apps, e.g. `blog/[slug].js`","  - You may notice new errors in these files since they were not being linted before","","- Better mono-repo support: Nested `node_modules/` folders are ignored by default [#1182](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1182)","","- Remove `eslint-plugin-standard` [#1316](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1316)","  - We migrated the remaining `no-callback-literal` rule into `eslint-plugin-node`","","### New rules","","_(Estimated % of affected standard users, based on test suite in parens)_","","- Require let or const instead of var As a result, the eslint team has decided to drop support for it.","    - To prevent breaking CI for projects which still support Node 6, `standard` silently passes when run by an unsupported version of Node.","  - **For `eslint-config-standard` users only:** Plugins are no longer affected by `eslint`'s location","    - Previously, ESLint loaded plugins relative to the location of the ESLint package itself. As a result, we suggested that users with global ESLint installations should also install plugins globally, and users with local ESLint installations should install plugins locally.","    - With ESLint v6, plugins should always be installed locally, even if ESLint was installed globally. More precisely, ESLint v6 resolves plugins relative to the end user’s project by default, and always resolves shareable configs and parsers relative to the location of the config file that imports them.","    - See [migrating to ESLint 6.0.0 for more information](https://eslint.org/docs/user-guide/migrating-to-6.0.0#-plugins-and-shareable-configs-are-no-longer-affected-by-eslints-location).","- ([spaced-comment](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/spaced-comment)) [#918](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/918)","","👏 Huge thanks to [@Flet](https://github.com/Flet) for putting together most of this","release!","","## [10.0.3] - 2017-08-06","","- Internal changes (incremented dependency versions)","","## [10.0.2] - 2017-04-14","","### Changed rules","","- Relax rule: Disallow import of modules using absolute paths ([import/no-absolute-path](https://github.com/benmosher/eslint-plugin-import/blob/master/docs/rules/no-absolute-path.md)) [#861](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/861)","  - This rule was responsible for up to 25% of the running time of `standard`, so we are disabling it until its performance improves.","","## [10.0.1] - 2017-04-06","","- Internal changes (incremented dependency versions)","","## [10.0.0] - 2017-04-04","","**`standard` just turned 10.0.0!** 🎉","","As with every new major release, there are lots of new rules in 10.0.0 designed to","help catch bugs and make programmer intent more explicit.","","`standard` is more popular than ever – **330,000 downloads per month!** It's even","more popular – **670,000 downloads per month** – if you include the","[shareable ESLint config](https://www.npmjs.com/package/eslint-config-standard)","that we also publish.","","The most important change in 10.0.0 is that **using deprecated Node.js APIs is now","considered an error**. It's finally time to update those dusty old APIs!","","Deprecated APIs are problematic because they may print warning messages in the","console in recent versions of Node.js. This often confuses users and leads to","unnecessary support tickets for project maintainers.","","Some deprecated APIs are even insecure (or at least prone to incorrect usage) which","can have serious security implications. For that reason, `standard` now considers","usage of `Buffer(num)` to be an error, since this function returns uninitialized","program memory which could contain confidential information like passwords or keys.","","Instead of `Buffer(num)`, consider using `Buffer.alloc(num)` or `Buffer.from(obj)`","which make the programmer's intent clearer. These functions exist in all currently","supported versions of Node.js, including Node.js 4.x. For more background,","[see this Node.js issue](https://github.com/nodejs/node/issues/4660).","","We also improved some rules to support common patterns in code bases that use","React, JSX, and Flow.","","When you upgrade, consider running `standard --fix` to automatically fix some of","the issues caught by this new version.","","### New features","","- Update ESLint from 3.15.x to 3.19.x.","- Node.js API: Add `standard.lintTextSync` method","","### New rules","","_(Estimated % of affected standard users, based on test suite in parens)_","","- Disallow using deprecated Node.js APIs ([node/no-deprecated-api](https://github.com/mysticatea/eslint-plugin-node/blob/master/docs/rules/no-deprecated-api.md)) [#693](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/693) [13%]","  - Ensures that code always runs without warnings on the latest versions of Node.js","  - Ensures that safe Buffer methods (`Buffer.from()`, `Buffer.alloc()`) are used instead of `Buffer()`","- Enforce callbacks always called with Node.js-style error first ([standard/no-callback-literal](https://github.com/xjamundx/eslint-plugin-standard#rules-explanations)) [#623](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/623) [3%]","  - Functions named `callback` or `cb` must be invoked with `null`, `undefined`, or an `Error` as the first argument","  - Disallows using a string instead of an `Error` object","  - Disallows confusing callbacks that do not follow the standard Node.js pattern","- Disallow any imports that come after non-import statements ([import/first](https://github.com/benmosher/eslint-plugin-import/blob/master/docs/rules/first.md)) [#806](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/806) [1%]","- Disallow unnecessary return await ([no-return-await](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-return-await)) [#695](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/695) [0%]","- Disallow comma-dangle in functions ([comma-dangle](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/comma-dangle)) [#787](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/787) [0%]","- Disallow repeated exports of names or defaults ([import/export](https://github.com/benmosher/eslint-plugin-import/blob/master/docs/rules/export.md)) [#806](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/806) [0%]","- Disallow import of modules using absolute paths ([import/no-absolute-path](https://github.com/benmosher/eslint-plugin-import/blob/master/docs/rules/no-absolute-path.md)) [#806](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/806) [0%]","- Disallow Webpack loader syntax in imports ([import/no-webpack-loader-syntax](https://github.com/benmosher/eslint-plugin-import/blob/master/docs/rules/no-webpack-loader-syntax.md)) [#806](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/806) [0%]","- Disallow comparing against -0 ([no-compare-neg-zero](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-compare-neg-zero)) [#812](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/812) [0%]","","### Changed rules","","- Relax rule: allow using `...rest` to omit properties from an object ([no-unused-vars](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-unused-vars)) [#800](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/800)","  - If you ever used","[`standard-format`](https://www.npmjs.com/package/standard-format)","and ran into issues with the lack of ES2015+ support, you'll be happy about","`--fix`.","","`standard --fix` is built into `standard` v8.0.0 for maximum convenience, it","supports ES2015, and it's lightweight (no additional dependencies since it's part","of ESLint which powers `standard`). Lots of problems are already fixable, and more","are getting added with each ESLint release.","","`standard` also outputs a message (\"Run `standard --fix` to automatically fix","some problems.\") when it detects problems that can be fixed automatically so you","can save time!","","With `standard` v8.0.0, we are also dropping support for Node.js versions prior to","v4. Node.js 0.10 and 0.12 are in maintenance mode and will be unsupported at the","end of 2016. Node.js 4 is the current LTS version. If you are using an older","version of Node.js, we recommend upgrading to at least Node.js 4 as soon as","possible. If you are unable to upgrade to Node.js 4 or higher, then we recommend","continuing to use `standard` v7.x until you are ready to upgrade Node.js.","","**Important:** We will not be updating the `standard` v7.x versions going forward.","All bug fixes and enhancements will land in `standard` v8.x.","","Full changelog below. [6.0.7] - 2016-02-18","","- Revert: Use install location of standard as eslint `cwd` (fixes [#429](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/429))","","## [6.0.6] - 2016-02-18","","- Use eslint 2.1.0","- Fix: Use install location of standard as eslint `cwd` (fixes [snazzy/#8](https://github.com/standard/snazzy/issues/8))","","## [6.0.5] - 2016-02-12","","- Use eslint 2.0.0 stable","","## [6.0.4] - 2016-02-07","","- Relax rule: Validate closing bracket location in JSX ([jsx-closing-bracket-location](https://github.com/yannickcr/eslint-plugin-react/blob/master/docs/rules/jsx-closing-bracket-location.md))","","## [6.0.3] - 2016-02-06","","- Fix \"Error: Cannot find module 'eslint-config-standard-jsx'\" with npm 2 (node 0.10, 0.12, 4)","","## [6.0.2] - 2016-02-06","","- Internal change: Remove .eslintrc file, and use inline config","","## [6.0.1] - 2016-02-05","","- Internal change: Move .eslintrc file to root folder","","## [6.0.0] - 2016-02-05","","The goal of this release is to make `standard` faster to install, and simpler to use.","","### Remove `standard-format` ([#340](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/340)) ([#397](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/397))","","- Eliminates 250 packages, and cuts install time in half!","- For npm 2, install time goes from 20 secs —\u003e 10 secs.","- For npm 3, install time goes from 24 secs —\u003e 12 secs.","- To continue using `standard-format`, just install it separately: `npm install -g standard-format`","","### React-specific linting rules are removed ([#351](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/351)) ([#367](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/367)) ([eslint-config-standard-react/#13](https://github.com/standard/eslint-config-standard-react/pull/13))","","- JSX is still supported, and it continues to be checked for style.","- There were only a few React-specific rules, but they made it extremely difficult for users of alternatives like `virtual-dom` or `deku`, and unecessarily tied `standard` to a single library.","- JSX rules come from `eslint-config-standard-jsx`. The `eslint-config-standard-react` dependency was removed.","","### New Rules","","_The percentage (%) of users that rule changes will effect, based on real-world testing of the top ~400 npm packages is denoted in brackets._","","- Disallow `__dirname`/`__filename` string concatenation ([#403](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/403)) ([no-path-concat](https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/no-path-concat)) [5%]","- Require parens in arrow function arguments ([#309](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/309)) ([arrow-parens](https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/arrow-parens.html)) [5%]","- Ensure that `new Promise()` is instantiated with the parameter names","  `resolve`, `reject` ([#282](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/282)) ([promise/param-names](https://github.com/xjamundx/eslint-plugin-promise#param-names)) [1%]","- Enforce Usage of Spacing in Template Strings ([template-curly-spacing](https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/template-curly-spacing)) [1%]","- Template strings are only allowed when necessary, i.e. template string features are being used (eslint got stricter: [eslint/eslint#5147](https://github.com/eslint/eslint/issues/5147)) [1%]","- Better dead code detection after conditional statements (eslint got stricter) [1%]","- Enforce spaces around `*` in `yield * something` ([#335](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/335)) ([yield-star-spacing](https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/yield-star-spacing)) [0%]","- Disallow labels on loops/switch statements too (made rule stricter) ([no-labels](https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/no-labels.html)) [0%]","- Disallow unnecessary constructor ([no-useless-constructor](https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/no-useless-constructor)) [0%]","- Disallow empty destructuring patterns ([no-empty-pattern](https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/no-empty-pattern)) [0%]","- Disallow Symbol Constructor ([no-new-symbol](https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/no-new-symbol)) [0%]","- Disallow Self Assignment ([no-self-assign](https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/no-self-assign)) [0%]","","### Removed Rules","","- `parseInt()` radix rule because ES5 fixes this issue ([#384](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/384)) ([radix](https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/radix.html)) [0%]","","### Expose eslint configuration via command line options and `package.json`","","For power users, it might be easier to use one of these new hooks instead of forking","`standard`, though that's still encouraged, too!","","- Set eslint \"plugins\" ([#386](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/386))","- Set eslint \"rules\" ([#367](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/367))","- Set eslint \"env\" ([#371](https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/371))","","To set custom ESLint plugins, rules, or envs, use the command line `--plugin`, `--rules`, and `--env` flags.","","In `package.json`, use the \"standard\" property:","","```json","{","  \"standard\": {","    \"plugins\": [ \"my-plugin\" ]","  }","}","```","","### Upgrade to ESLint v2","","- There may be slight behavior changes to existing rules. When possible, we've noted these in the \"New Rules\" and \"Removed Rules\" section.","","### Improve test suite","","- Rule changes can be tested against every package on npm. For sanity, this is limited to packages with at least 4 dependents. Around 400 packages.","","### Known Issues","","- Using prerelease eslint version (2.0.0-rc.0). There may be breaking changes before the stable release.","- `no-return-assign` behavior changed with arrow functions ([eslint/eslint#5150](https://github.com/eslint/eslint/issues/5150))","","### Relevant diffs","","- standard ([v5.4.1...v6.0.0](https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v5.4.1...v6.0.0))","- eslint-config-standard ([v4.4.0...v5.0.0](https://github.com/standard/eslint-config-standard/compare/v4.4.0...v5.0.0))","- eslint-config-standard-jsx ([v1.0.0](https://github.com/standard/eslint-config-standard-jsx/commit/47d5e248e2e078eb87619493999e3e74d4b7e70e))","- standard-engine ([v2.2.4...v3.2.1](https://github.com/Flet/standard-engine/compare/v2.2.4...v3.2.1))","","## [5.4.1] - 2015-11-16","","[view diff](https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v5.4.0...v5.4.1)","","### Fixed","","- Fix for `standard-engine` change. <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">[17.1.0] - 2023-05-29</h2><a id="user-content-1710---2023-05-29" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: [17.1.0] - 2023-05-29" href="#1710---2023-05-29"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">[17.0.0] - 2022-04-20</h2><a id="user-content-1700---2022-04-20" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: [17.0.0] - 2022-04-20" href="#1700---2022-04-20"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We're super excited to announce <code>standard</code> 17!</p>
<p dir="auto">This major release fully focuses on getting in sync with the wider ESLint ecosystem
and doesn't in itself introduce any new rules or features.</p>
<p dir="auto">When you upgrade, consider running <code>standard --fix</code> to automatically format your
code to match the current set of rules.</p>
<p dir="auto">This is the first release by two of our <code>standard</code> co-maintainers @Divlo and @voxpelli. Buy them a cake if you run into them, thanks for getting this release out!</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Major changes</h3><a id="user-content-major-changes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Major changes" href="#major-changes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>eslint-config-node</code> has been replaced with the up to date fork <code>eslint-config-n</code>. If you have used comments like <code>// eslint-disable-line node/no-deprecated-api</code> you now have to reference the <code>n/</code> rules instead.</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/standard/eslint-config-standard/pull/166" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/standard/eslint-config-standard/pull/166/hovercard"><code>object-shorthand</code> rule</a> (as warning)</li>
<li>Use of ESLint 8, which allows for support for all of the latest syntax that ESLint 8 includes, such as top level <code>await</code> #1548 #1775</li>
<li><code>--verbose</code> by default</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Changed features</h3><a id="user-content-changed-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Changed features" href="#changed-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Update <code>eslint</code> from <code>~7.18.0</code> to <code>^8.13.0</code></li>
<li>Update <code>eslint-config-standard</code> from <code>16.0.3</code> to <code>17.0.0</code> to adapt to ESLint 8</li>
<li>Update <code>eslint-config-standard-jsx</code> from <code>10.0.0</code> to <code>^11.0.0</code> to adapt to ESLint 8</li>
<li>Update <code>standard-engine</code> from <code>^14</code> to <code>^15.0.0</code> to adapt to ESLint 8, see <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard-engine/blob/master/CHANGELOG.md#1500-0-2021-11-30">its <code>CHANGELOG</code></a></li>
<li>Move from <code>eslint-plugin-node@~11.1.0</code> to <code>eslint-plugin-n@^15.1.0</code> to adapt to ESLint 8</li>
<li>Update <code>eslint-plugin-import</code> from <code>~2.24.2</code> to <code>^2.26.0</code></li>
<li>Update <code>eslint-plugin-promise</code> from <code>~5.1.0</code> to <code>^6.0.0</code></li>
<li>Update <code>eslint-plugin-react</code> from <code>~7.25.1</code> to <code>^7.28.0</code></li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">[17.0.0-0] - 2022-01-31</h2><a id="user-content-1700-0---2022-01-31" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: [17.0.0-0] - 2022-01-31" href="#1700-0---2022-01-31"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We're finally able to offer a pre-release of ESLint 8 based <code>standard</code> 17!</p>
<p dir="auto">This major release fully focuses on getting in sync with the wider ESLint ecosystem
and doesn't in itself introduce any new rules or features.</p>
<p dir="auto">This pre-release exists to test out the ESLint 8 related changes and discover
possible backwards incompatible changes that comes with it and mitigate
unintended such before a stable release.</p>
<p dir="auto">When you upgrade, consider running <code>standard --fix</code> to automatically format your
code to match the current set of rules.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Changed features</h3><a id="user-content-changed-features-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Changed features" href="#changed-features-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Update <code>eslint</code> from <code>~7.18.0</code> to <code>^8.8.0</code></li>
<li>Update <code>eslint-config-standard</code> from <code>16.0.3</code> to <code>17.0.0-0</code> to adapt to ESLint 8</li>
<li>Update <code>eslint-config-standard-jsx</code> from <code>10.0.0</code> to <code>11.0.0-0</code> to adapt to ESLint 8</li>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v16.0.0...v16.0.1">16.0.1</a> - 2020-10-30</h2><a id="user-content-1601---2020-10-30" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 16.0.1 - 2020-10-30" href="#1601---2020-10-30"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Introduce "warning" system for disruptive rules (read more below)</li>
<li>Change rule to a "warning": Require let or const instead of var (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-var" rel="nofollow">no-var</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/633" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/633/hovercard">#633</a></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><code>standard</code> treats all rule violations as errors, which means that <code>standard</code>
will exit with a non-zero (error) exit code.</p>
<p dir="auto">However, we may occasionally release a new major version of <code>standard</code>
which changes a rule that affects the majority of <code>standard</code> users (for example,
transitioning from <code>var</code> to <code>let</code>/<code>const</code>). We do this only when we think the
advantage is worth the cost and only when the rule is
<a href="https://standardjs.com/#is-there-an-automatic-formatter" rel="nofollow">auto-fixable</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">In these situations, we have a "transition period" where the rule change is only
a "warning". Warnings don't cause <code>standard</code> to return a non-zero (error)
exit code. However, a warning message will still print to the console. During
the transition period, <code>using standard --fix</code> will update your code so that it's
ready for the next major version.</p>
<p dir="auto">The slow and careful approach is what we strive for with <code>standard</code>. We're
generally extremely conservative in enforcing the usage of new language
features. We want using <code>standard</code> to be light and fun and so we're careful
about making changes that may get in your way. As always, you can
<a href="https://standardjs.com/#how-do-i-disable-a-rule" rel="nofollow">disable a rule</a> at any time, if necessary.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v15.0.1...v16.0.0">16.0.0</a> - 2020-10-28</h2><a id="user-content-1600---2020-10-28" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 16.0.0 - 2020-10-28" href="#1600---2020-10-28"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We're super excited to announce <code>standard</code> 16!</p>
<p dir="auto">As with every new major release, there are lots of new rules in 16.0.0 designed
to help catch bugs and make programmer intent more explicit. This release brings
better performance, tons of bug fixes, improved JSX, React ⚛️, and Next.js support!</p>
<p dir="auto">When you upgrade, consider running <code>standard --fix</code> to automatically format your
code to match the newly added rules.</p>
<p dir="auto">❤️ If you enjoy StandardJS and want to support future releases, please
<a href="https://github.com/users/feross/sponsorship">support Feross</a>!</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">New features</h3><a id="user-content-new-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: New features" href="#new-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">🏎 Better performance: the filesystem doesn't need to be traversed multiple times! <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1023" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1023/hovercard">#1023</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Massive improvements (on the order of minutes!) for projects with huge folders which are are ignored with <code>.gitignore</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">🌟 Support the <code>.gitignore</code> ignore syntax from the command line <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1117" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1117/hovercard">#1117</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>In older versions, the command <code>standard src</code> would not lint the <code>src/</code> folder</li>
<li>Instead, a glob pattern like <code>standard src/**/*.js</code> was required</li>
<li>This is now fixed! You can run <code>standard src</code> to lint the <code>src/</code> folder!</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">🌟 Support relative paths from the command line in more situations (e.g. <code>standard ../src/*.js</code>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1384" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1384/hovercard">#1384</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">🌟 New <code>extensions</code> option for linting additional extensions besides <code>.js</code>, <code>.jsx</code>, <code>.mjs</code>, and <code>.cjs</code></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Can be configured with the <code>--ext</code> command line flag or in <code>package.json</code>:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Example:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="standard --ext .ts"><pre>standard --ext .ts</pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;standard&quot;: {
    &quot;extensions&quot;: [&quot;.ts&quot;]
  }
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"standard"</span>: {
    <span class="pl-ent">"extensions"</span>: [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>.ts<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>]
  }
}</pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">🌟 New cache directory location, respecting <code>XDG_CACHE_HOME</code> preference, with fallback to <code>~/.cache/standard</code> <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard-engine/pull/214" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard-engine/pull/214/hovercard">standard-engine/#214</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Changed features</h3><a id="user-content-changed-features-2" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Changed features" href="#changed-features-2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Update <code>eslint</code> from <code>~7.11.0</code> to <code>~7.12.1</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Update <code>standard-engine</code> from <code>^12</code> to <code>^14</code></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Fix inaccurate <code>--help</code> command which indicates that <code>bundle.js</code> is automatically ignored when it is not anymore <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard-engine/pull/224" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard-engine/pull/224/hovercard">standard-engine/#224</a></li>
<li>Remove <code>deglob</code> package and use built-in ESLint folder-traversal support</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Paths with square brackets (e.g. <code>[</code> and <code>]</code>) are no longer skipped <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1333" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1333/hovercard">#1333</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>This pattern is particularly common in Next.js apps, e.g. <code>blog/[slug].js</code></li>
<li>You may notice new errors in these files since they were not being linted before</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Better mono-repo support: Nested <code>node_modules/</code> folders are ignored by default <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1182" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1182/hovercard">#1182</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Remove <code>eslint-plugin-standard</code> <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1316" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1316/hovercard">#1316</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We migrated the remaining <code>no-callback-literal</code> rule into <code>eslint-plugin-node</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v15.0.0...v15.0.1">15.0.1</a> - 2020-10-27</h2><a id="user-content-1501---2020-10-27" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 15.0.1 - 2020-10-27" href="#1501---2020-10-27"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v14.3.4...v15.0.0">15.0.0</a> - 2020-10-21</h2><a id="user-content-1500---2020-10-21" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 15.0.0 - 2020-10-21" href="#1500---2020-10-21"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We're super excited to announce <code>standard</code> 15!</p>
<p dir="auto">As with every new major release, there are lots of new rules in 15.0.0 designed
to help catch bugs and make programmer intent more explicit. This release brings
support for ES 2021, the latest version of the ECMAScript specification, as well
as many quality-of-life improvements, including ESLint v7.</p>
<p dir="auto">When you upgrade, consider running <code>standard --fix</code> to automatically format your
code to match the newly added rules.</p>
<p dir="auto">❤️ If you enjoy StandardJS and want to support future releases, check out
Feross's <a href="https://github.com/users/feross/sponsorship">GitHub Sponsors page</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">New features</h3><a id="user-content-new-features-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: New features" href="#new-features-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Support ES 2021, the latest version of the ECMAScript specification, which includes support for <a href="https://github.com/tc39/proposal-logical-assignment">logical assignment operators</a> and <a href="https://github.com/tc39/proposal-numeric-separator">numeric separators</a> <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1551" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1551/hovercard">#1551</a></li>
<li>Support ES 2020 features such as <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Operators/Optional_chaining" rel="nofollow">optional chaining</a>, the <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Operators/Nullish_coalescing_operator" rel="nofollow">nullish coalescing operator</a>, <code>export * as ns from 'source'</code>, and <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Statements/import.meta" rel="nofollow"><code>import.meta</code></a>.</li>
<li>Support global variables from ES 2017 (<code>Atomics</code>, <code>SharedArrayBuffer</code>), ES 2020 (<code>BigInt</code>, <code>BigInt64Array</code>, <code>BigUint64Array</code>, <code>globalThis</code>), and ES 2021 (<code>FinalizationRegistry</code>, <code>WeakRef</code>). <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1436" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1436/hovercard">#1436</a> <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1557" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1557/hovercard">#1557</a> <a href="https://github.com/standard/eslint-config-standard/pull/156" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/standard/eslint-config-standard/pull/156/hovercard">eslint-config-standard/#156</a></li>
<li>The documentation is now available in Indonesian 🇮🇩! <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/pull/1544" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/pull/1544/hovercard">#1544</a>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Thanks to <a href="https://github.com/yoga1234">@yoga1234</a> for the excellent work!</li>
<li>Other community contributed translations exist in Spanish, French, Italian, Japanese, Korean, Portuguese, Simplified Chinese, and Taiwanese Mandarin.</li>
<li>More translations are always welcome!</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Changed features</h3><a id="user-content-changed-features-3" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Changed features" href="#changed-features-3"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>BREAKING: Node.js 8 is no longer supported
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Node.js 8 is EOL and will no longer be receiving security updates.</li>
<li>To prevent breaking CI for projects which still support Node 8, <code>standard</code> silently passes when run by an unsupported version of Node</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Update <code>eslint</code> from <code>~6.8.0</code> to <code>~7.11.0</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">New rules</h3><a id="user-content-new-rules-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: New rules" href="#new-rules-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>Require indentation for values of ternary expressions (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/indent" rel="nofollow">indent</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/927" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/927/hovercard">#927</a> [4%]</li>
<li>Enforce newlines between operands of ternary expressions if the expression spans multiple lines (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/multiline-ternary" rel="nofollow">multiline-ternary</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1558" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1558/hovercard">#1558</a> [3%]</li>
<li>Disallow loops with a body that allows only one iteration (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-unreachable-loop" rel="nofollow">no-unreachable-loop</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1556" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1556/hovercard">#1556</a> [0%]</li>
<li>Disallow useless backreferences in regular expressions (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-useless-backreference" rel="nofollow">no-useless-backreference</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1554" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1554/hovercard">#1554</a> [0%]</li>
<li>Enforce default clauses in switch statements to be last (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/default-case-last" rel="nofollow">default-case-last</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1553" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1553/hovercard">#1553</a> [0%]</li>
<li>Disallow Number Literals That Lose Precision (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-loss-of-precision" rel="nofollow">no-loss-of-precision</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1552" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1552/hovercard">#1552</a> [0%]</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v13.1.0...v14.0.0">14.0.0</a> - 2019-08-19</h2><a id="user-content-1400---2019-08-19" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 14.0.0 - 2019-08-19" href="#1400---2019-08-19"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We're super excited to announce <code>standard</code> 14!</p>
<p dir="auto">As with every new major release, there are lots of new rules in 14.0.0 designed
to help catch bugs and make programmer intent more explicit. This release brings
support for ES 2019, the latest version of the ECMAScript specification, as well
as many quality-of-life improvements for users who use tagged template strings,
JSX, and <code>.mjs</code> files for ES modules.</p>
<p dir="auto">When you upgrade, consider running <code>standard --fix</code> to automatically format your
code to match the newly added rules.</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>standard</code> keeps growing! The latest stats show that <code>standard</code> and
<code>eslint-standard-*</code> shareable configs are depended upon by <strong>318,512 GitHub
repositories</strong> and <strong>33,349 public npm packages</strong>. Thanks for spreading the
word!</p>
<p dir="auto">We now have a <a href="https://discord.gg/ZegqCBr" rel="nofollow">Discord server</a>. Come chat with the
maintainers, ask questions, and get help from the community!</p>
<p dir="auto">❤️ If you enjoy StandardJS and want to support future releases, check out
Feross's <a href="https://github.com/users/feross/sponsorship">GitHub Sponsors page</a>.
GitHub is matching donations, so your dollars go twice as far! 🚀</p>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>Require Dot Notation Whenever Possible (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/dot-notation" rel="nofollow">dot-notation</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1344" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1344/hovercard">#1344</a> [6%]</li>
<li>Require consistent line breaks inside braces (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/object-curly-newline" rel="nofollow">object-curly-newline</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/782" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/782/hovercard">#782</a> [1%]</li>
<li>Disallow template literals when placeholders or tagged template features are not used. (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/quotes" rel="nofollow">quotes</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/838" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/838/hovercard">#838</a> <a href="https://github.com/standard/eslint-config-standard/pull/151" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/standard/eslint-config-standard/pull/151/hovercard">eslint-config-standard/#151</a> [1%]</li>
<li>Disallow lexical declarations in case/default clauses (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-case-declarations" rel="nofollow">no-case-declarations</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1211" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1211/hovercard">#1211</a> <a href="https://github.com/standard/eslint-config-standard/pull/137" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/standard/eslint-config-standard/pull/137/hovercard">eslint-config-standard/#137</a> [1%]</li>
<li>Require the first JSX property to be placed on a new line if the JSX tag takes up multiple lines and there are multiple properties (<a href="https://github.com/yannickcr/eslint-plugin-react/blob/master/docs/rules/jsx-first-prop-new-line.md">react/jsx-first-prop-new-line</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/696" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/696/hovercard">#696</a> [1%]</li>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v12.0.1...v13.0.0">13.0.0</a> - 2019-07-10</h2><a id="user-content-1300---2019-07-10" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 13.0.0 - 2019-07-10" href="#1300---2019-07-10"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Welcome to the latest version of <code>standard</code>!</p>
<p dir="auto">As with every new major release, there are lots of new rules in 13.0.0 designed
to help catch bugs and make programmer intent more explicit.</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>standard</code> is more popular than ever – <strong>640,000 downloads per month!</strong> It's
even more popular – <strong>3,000,000 downloads per month</strong> – if you include the
<a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/eslint-config-standard" rel="nofollow">ESLint configuration</a>
that we also publish (for advanced users).</p>
<p dir="auto">When you upgrade, consider running <code>standard --fix</code> to automatically format your code to match the newly added rules.</p>
<p dir="auto">❤️ If you enjoy StandardJS and want to support future releases, check out Feross's <a href="https://github.com/users/feross/sponsorship">GitHub Sponsors page</a>. GitHub is matching donations, so your dollars go twice as far! 🚀</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">New features</h3><a id="user-content-new-features-3" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: New features" href="#new-features-3"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Update <code>eslint</code> from <code>~5.16.0</code> to <code>~6.0.1</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>BREAKING: Node.js 6 is no longer supported
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Node.js 6 is EOL and will no longer be receiving security updates. As a result, the eslint team has decided to drop support for it.</li>
<li>To prevent breaking CI for projects which still support Node 6, <code>standard</code> silently passes when run by an unsupported version of Node.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>For <code>eslint-config-standard</code> users only:</strong> Plugins are no longer affected by <code>eslint</code>'s location
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Previously, ESLint loaded plugins relative to the location of the ESLint package itself. As a result, we suggested that users with global ESLint installations should also install plugins globally, and users with local ESLint installations should install plugins locally.</li>
<li>With ESLint v6, plugins should always be installed locally, even if ESLint was installed globally. More precisely, ESLint v6 resolves plugins relative to the end user’s project by default, and always resolves shareable configs and parsers relative to the location of the config file that imports them.</li>
<li>See <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/user-guide/migrating-to-6.0.0#-plugins-and-shareable-configs-are-no-longer-affected-by-eslints-location" rel="nofollow">migrating to ESLint 6.0.0 for more information</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The documentation is now available in Japanese 🇯🇵!
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Thanks to <a href="https://github.com/munierujp">@munierujp</a> for the excellent work!</li>
<li>Other community contributed translations exist in Spanish, French, Italian, Korean, Portuguese, Simplified Chinese, and Taiwanese Mandarin.</li>
<li>More translations are always welcome!</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Update <code>eslint-plugin-promise</code> from <code>~4.0.0</code> to <code>~4.2.1</code></li>
<li>Update <code>eslint-plugin-node</code> from <code>~7.0.1</code> to <code>~9.1.0</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">New rules</h3><a id="user-content-new-rules-3" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: New rules" href="#new-rules-3"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><em>(Estimated % of affected standard users, based on test suite in parens)</em></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Disallow spaces inside of array brackets (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/array-bracket-spacing" rel="nofollow">array-bracket-spacing</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1203" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1203/hovercard">#1203</a> <a href="https://github.com/standard/eslint-config-standard/pull/131" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/standard/eslint-config-standard/pull/131/hovercard">eslint-config-standard/#131</a> [14%]</li>

<li>Disallow unnecessary catch clauses (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-useless-catch" rel="nofollow">no-useless-catch</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/1312" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/1312/hovercard">#1312</a> [0%]</li>

</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">New features</h3><a id="user-content-new-features-4" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: New features" href="#new-features-4"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<li>Update <code>eslint</code> from <code>~4.19.0</code> to <code>~5.4.0</code>.
<ul dir="auto">

<li>Lots of minor changes to rules to catch more edge cases!</li>
</ul>
</li>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>Other community contributed translations exist in Spanish, Italian, Korean, Portuguese, Simplified Chinese, and Taiwanese Mandarin.</li>
<li>More translations are welcome!</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">New rules</h3><a id="user-content-new-rules-4" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: New rules" href="#new-rules-4"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Changed rules</h3><a id="user-content-changed-rules-4" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Changed rules" href="#changed-rules-4"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
