<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v10.0.3...v11.0.0">11.0.0</a> - 2018-02-18</h2><a id="user-content-1100---2018-02-18" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 11.0.0 - 2018-02-18" href="#1100---2018-02-18"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This release has no new rules, but it does update to the latest version of <code>eslint</code>,
version 4, which has some significant changes to existing rules. Most updates make
the indentation rules more strict.</p>
<p dir="auto">Thankfully, most users will just need to run <code>standard --fix</code> to update code to be
compliant.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">New features</h3><a id="user-content-new-features-5" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: New features" href="#new-features-5"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Update <code>eslint</code> from ~3.19.0 to ~4.18.0.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The <code>indent</code> rule is more strict.</li>
<li>The <code>padded-blocks</code> rule is more strict.</li>
<li>The <code>space-before-function-paren</code> rule is more strict.</li>
<li>The <code>no-multi-spaces</code> rule is more strict.</li>
<li>Minor improvements to:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>no-extra-parens</code>,</li>
<li><code>no-unexpected-multiline</code>,</li>
<li><code>no-regex-spaces</code>, and</li>
<li><code>space-unary-ops</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Update <code>eslint-plugin-import</code> from <code>~2.2.0</code> to <code>~2.8.0</code></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Updated for eslint 4.0 compatibility.</li>
<li>Various small bug fixes included related to <code>import/*</code> rules.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Update <code>eslint-plugin-node</code> from <code>~4.2.2</code> to <code>~6.0.0</code></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The <code>no-deprecated-api</code> rule is updated with Node.js 8 support and improved
Node 6 support.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Upodate <code>eslint-plugin-promise</code> from <code>~3.5.0</code> to <code>~3.6.0</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Update <code>eslint-plugin-react</code> from <code>~6.10.0</code> to <code>~7.6.1</code></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Fix <code>jsx-indent</code> crash</li>
<li>Fix <code>jsx-indent</code> indentation calculation with nested JSX.</li>
<li>Fix <code>jsx-no-undef</code> will not check the global scope by default.</li>
<li>Fix <code>jsx-curly-spacing</code> newline with object literals bug.</li>
<li>Fix <code>jsx-curly-spacing</code> schema incompatibility with ESLint 4.2.0.</li>
<li>Fix alignment bug in <code>jsx-indent</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Changed rules</h3><a id="user-content-changed-rules-5" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Changed rules" href="#changed-rules-5"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Relax rule: Don't mark Rails Asset Pipeline comments (comments that start with <code>//=</code>)
as errors. (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/spaced-comment" rel="nofollow">spaced-comment</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/918" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/918/hovercard">#918</a></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">👏 Huge thanks to <a href="https://github.com/Flet">@Flet</a> for putting together most of this
release!</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v10.0.0...v10.0.1">10.0.1</a> - 2017-04-06</h2><a id="user-content-1001---2017-04-06" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 10.0.1 - 2017-04-06" href="#1001---2017-04-06"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v9.0.2...v10.0.0">10.0.0</a> - 2017-04-04</h2><a id="user-content-1000---2017-04-04" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 10.0.0 - 2017-04-04" href="#1000---2017-04-04"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>standard</code> just turned 10.0.0!</strong> 🎉</p>
<p dir="auto">As with every new major release, there are lots of new rules in 10.0.0 designed to
help catch bugs and make programmer intent more explicit.</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>standard</code> is more popular than ever – <strong>330,000 downloads per month!</strong> It's even
more popular – <strong>670,000 downloads per month</strong> – if you include the
<a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/eslint-config-standard" rel="nofollow">shareable ESLint config</a>
that we also publish.</p>
<p dir="auto">The most important change in 10.0.0 is that <strong>using deprecated Node.js APIs is now
considered an error</strong>. It's finally time to update those dusty old APIs!</p>
<p dir="auto">Deprecated APIs are problematic because they may print warning messages in the
console in recent versions of Node.js. This often confuses users and leads to
unnecessary support tickets for project maintainers.</p>
<p dir="auto">Some deprecated APIs are even insecure (or at least prone to incorrect usage) which
can have serious security implications. For that reason, <code>standard</code> now considers
usage of <code>Buffer(num)</code> to be an error, since this function returns uninitialized
program memory which could contain confidential information like passwords or keys.</p>
<p dir="auto">Instead of <code>Buffer(num)</code>, consider using <code>Buffer.alloc(num)</code> or <code>Buffer.from(obj)</code>
which make the programmer's intent clearer. These functions exist in all currently
supported versions of Node.js, including Node.js 4.x. For more background,
<a href="https://github.com/nodejs/node/issues/4660" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/nodejs/node/issues/4660/hovercard">see this Node.js issue</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">We also improved some rules to support common patterns in code bases that use
React, JSX, and Flow.</p>
<p dir="auto">When you upgrade, consider running <code>standard --fix</code> to automatically fix some of
the issues caught by this new version.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">New features</h3><a id="user-content-new-features-6" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: New features" href="#new-features-6"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Update ESLint from 3.15.x to 3.19.x.</li>
<li>Node.js API: Add <code>standard.lintTextSync</code> method</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">New rules</h3><a id="user-content-new-rules-5" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: New rules" href="#new-rules-5"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><em>(Estimated % of affected standard users, based on test suite in parens)</em></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Disallow using deprecated Node.js APIs (<a href="https://github.com/mysticatea/eslint-plugin-node/blob/master/docs/rules/no-deprecated-api.md">node/no-deprecated-api</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/693" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/693/hovercard">#693</a> [13%]
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Ensures that code always runs without warnings on the latest versions of Node.js</li>
<li>Ensures that safe Buffer methods (<code>Buffer.from()</code>, <code>Buffer.alloc()</code>) are used instead of <code>Buffer()</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Enforce callbacks always called with Node.js-style error first (<a href="https://github.com/xjamundx/eslint-plugin-standard#rules-explanations">standard/no-callback-literal</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/623" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/623/hovercard">#623</a> [3%]
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Functions named <code>callback</code> or <code>cb</code> must be invoked with <code>null</code>, <code>undefined</code>, or an <code>Error</code> as the first argument</li>
<li>Disallows using a string instead of an <code>Error</code> object</li>
<li>Disallows confusing callbacks that do not follow the standard Node.js pattern</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Disallow any imports that come after non-import statements (<a href="https://github.com/benmosher/eslint-plugin-import/blob/master/docs/rules/first.md">import/first</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/806" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/806/hovercard">#806</a> [1%]</li>
<li>Disallow unnecessary return await (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-return-await" rel="nofollow">no-return-await</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/695" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/695/hovercard">#695</a> [0%]</li>
<li>Disallow comma-dangle in functions (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/comma-dangle" rel="nofollow">comma-dangle</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/787" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/787/hovercard">#787</a> [0%]</li>
<li>Disallow repeated exports of names or defaults (<a href="https://github.com/benmosher/eslint-plugin-import/blob/master/docs/rules/export.md">import/export</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/806" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/806/hovercard">#806</a> [0%]</li>
<li>Disallow import of modules using absolute paths (<a href="https://github.com/benmosher/eslint-plugin-import/blob/master/docs/rules/no-absolute-path.md">import/no-absolute-path</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/806" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/806/hovercard">#806</a> [0%]</li>
<li>Disallow Webpack loader syntax in imports (<a href="https://github.com/benmosher/eslint-plugin-import/blob/master/docs/rules/no-webpack-loader-syntax.md">import/no-webpack-loader-syntax</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/806" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/806/hovercard">#806</a> [0%]</li>
<li>Disallow comparing against -0 (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-compare-neg-zero" rel="nofollow">no-compare-neg-zero</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/812" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/812/hovercard">#812</a> [0%]</li>
</ul>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>Relax rule: allow using <code>...rest</code> to omit properties from an object (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-unused-vars" rel="nofollow">no-unused-vars</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/800" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/800/hovercard">#800</a>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>This is a common and useful pattern in React/JSX apps!</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Relax rule: allow Flow <code>import type</code> statements (<a href="https://github.com/benmosher/eslint-plugin-import/blob/master/docs/rules/no-duplicates.md">import/no-duplicates</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/599" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/599/hovercard">#599</a>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>These are no longer considered to be "duplicate imports"</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Relax rule: Treat <code>process.exit()</code> the same as <code>throw</code> in code path analysis (<a href="https://github.com/mysticatea/eslint-plugin-node/blob/master/docs/rules/process-exit-as-throw.md">node/process-exit-as-throw</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/699" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/699/hovercard">#699</a>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Makes certain other rules work better and give fewer false positives</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Relax rule: allow Unnecessary Labels (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-extra-label" rel="nofollow">no-extra-label</a>)
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Redundant, since "no-labels" is already enabled, which is more restrictive</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v8.6.0...v9.0.0">9.0.0</a> - 2017-02-28</h2><a id="user-content-900---2017-02-28" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 9.0.0 - 2017-02-28" href="#900---2017-02-28"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">It's time for a new major version of <code>standard</code>! As usual, this release contains a
bunch of awesomeness to help you keep your code in tip-top shape!</p>
<p dir="auto">We've added several new rules designed to <strong>catch potential programmer errors</strong>
(i.e. bugs), as well as rules to make programmer intent <strong>more explicit</strong> in
certain circumstances.</p>
<p dir="auto">This release continues our trend of tightening up rules so that, wherever possible,
there's one "right" way to do things. This design goal is intended to reduce the
time that teams and maintainers spend giving code review feedback in pull requests.</p>
<p dir="auto">When you upgrade, consider running <code>standard --fix</code> to automatically fix some of the
errors caught by the new rules in this version.</p>
<p dir="auto"><em>Note: If you use the Chai test framework, you will need to make some changes to
your tests to improve their robustness. <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/690#issuecomment-278533482" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/690/hovercard">Read about the changes you need to make</a>.</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">New features</h3><a id="user-content-new-features-7" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: New features" href="#new-features-7"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<li>Update ESLint from 3.10.x to 3.15.x</li>
<li>3 additional rules are now fixable with <code>standard --fix</code></li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v8.2.0...v8.3.0">8.3.0</a> - 2016-09-29</h2><a id="user-content-830---2016-09-29" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 8.3.0 - 2016-09-29" href="#830---2016-09-29"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The last release (<code>8.2.0</code>) added ES7 support. This release (<code>8.3.0</code>) adds ES8
support ...just 3 days later!</p>
<p dir="auto">This release should eliminate the need to specify <code>babel-eslint</code> as a custom
parser, since <code>standard</code> can now parse ES8 (i.e. ES2017) syntax out of the box.
That means <code>async</code> and <code>await</code> will just work.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Support ES8 (i.e. ES2017) syntax.</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v7.1.2...v8.0.0">8.0.0</a> - 2016-08-23</h2><a id="user-content-800---2016-08-23" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 8.0.0 - 2016-08-23" href="#800---2016-08-23"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This release contains a bunch of goodies, including new rules that catch potential
programmer errors (i.e. bugs) and enforce additional code consistency.</p>
<p dir="auto">However, the best feature is surely the new <code>--fix</code> command line flag to
automatically fix problems. If you ever used
<a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/standard-format" rel="nofollow"><code>standard-format</code></a>
and ran into issues with the lack of ES2015+ support, you'll be happy about
<code>--fix</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>standard --fix</code> is built into <code>standard</code> v8.0.0 for maximum convenience, it
supports ES2015, and it's lightweight (no additional dependencies since it's part
of ESLint which powers <code>standard</code>). Lots of problems are already fixable, and more
are getting added with each ESLint release.</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>standard</code> also outputs a message ("Run <code>standard --fix</code> to automatically fix
some problems.") when it detects problems that can be fixed automatically so you
can save time!</p>
<p dir="auto">With <code>standard</code> v8.0.0, we are also dropping support for Node.js versions prior to
v4. Node.js 0.10 and 0.12 are in maintenance mode and will be unsupported at the
end of 2016. Node.js 4 is the current LTS version. If you are using an older
version of Node.js, we recommend upgrading to at least Node.js 4 as soon as
possible. If you are unable to upgrade to Node.js 4 or higher, then we recommend
continuing to use <code>standard</code> v7.x until you are ready to upgrade Node.js.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Important:</strong> We will not be updating the <code>standard</code> v7.x versions going forward.
All bug fixes and enhancements will land in <code>standard</code> v8.x.</p>
<p dir="auto">Full changelog below. Cheers!</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">New features</h3><a id="user-content-new-features-8" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: New features" href="#new-features-8"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Upgrade to ESLint v3 (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/user-guide/migrating-to-3.0.0" rel="nofollow">https://eslint.org/docs/user-guide/migrating-to-3.0.0</a>) <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/pull/565" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/pull/565/hovercard">#565</a>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>BREAKING:</strong> Drop support for node &lt; 4 (this was a decision made by the ESLint team)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Expose ESLint's <code>--fix</code> command line flag <a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/540" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/540/hovercard">#540</a> <a href="https://github.com/Flet/standard-engine/issues/107" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard-engine/issues/107/hovercard">standard-engine/#107</a>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Lightweight, no additional dependencies, fixes dozens of rules automatically</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v5.4.1...v6.0.0">6.0.0</a> - 2016-02-05</h2><a id="user-content-600---2016-02-05" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 6.0.0 - 2016-02-05" href="#600---2016-02-05"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The goal of this release is to make <code>standard</code> faster to install, and simpler to use.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Remove <code>standard-format</code> (<a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/340" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/340/hovercard">#340</a>) (<a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/397" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/pull/397/hovercard">#397</a>)</h3><a id="user-content-remove-standard-format-340-397" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Remove standard-format (#340) (#397)" href="#remove-standard-format-340-397"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Eliminates 250 packages, and cuts install time in half!</li>
<li>For npm 2, install time goes from 20 secs —&gt; 10 secs.</li>
<li>For npm 3, install time goes from 24 secs —&gt; 12 secs.</li>
<li>To continue using <code>standard-format</code>, just install it separately: <code>npm install -g standard-format</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">React-specific linting rules are removed (<a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/351" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/351/hovercard">#351</a>) (<a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/367" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/367/hovercard">#367</a>) (<a href="https://github.com/standard/eslint-config-standard-react/pull/13" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/standard/eslint-config-standard-react/pull/13/hovercard">eslint-config-standard-react/#13</a>)</h3><a id="user-content-react-specific-linting-rules-are-removed-351-367-eslint-config-standard-react13" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: React-specific linting rules are removed (#351) (#367) (eslint-config-standard-react/#13)" href="#react-specific-linting-rules-are-removed-351-367-eslint-config-standard-react13"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>JSX is still supported, and it continues to be checked for style.</li>
<li>There were only a few React-specific rules, but they made it extremely difficult for users of alternatives like <code>virtual-dom</code> or <code>deku</code>, and unecessarily tied <code>standard</code> to a single library.</li>
<li>JSX rules come from <code>eslint-config-standard-jsx</code>. The <code>eslint-config-standard-react</code> dependency was removed.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">New Rules</h3><a id="user-content-new-rules-9" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: New Rules" href="#new-rules-9"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><em>The percentage (%) of users that rule changes will effect, based on real-world testing of the top ~400 npm packages is denoted in brackets.</em></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Disallow <code>__dirname</code>/<code>__filename</code> string concatenation (<a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/403" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/403/hovercard">#403</a>) (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/no-path-concat" rel="nofollow">no-path-concat</a>) [5%]</li>
<li>Require parens in arrow function arguments (<a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/309" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/309/hovercard">#309</a>) (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/arrow-parens.html" rel="nofollow">arrow-parens</a>) [5%]</li>
<li>Ensure that <code>new Promise()</code> is instantiated with the parameter names
<code>resolve</code>, <code>reject</code> (<a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/282" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/282/hovercard">#282</a>) (<a href="https://github.com/xjamundx/eslint-plugin-promise#param-names">promise/param-names</a>) [1%]</li>
<li>Enforce Usage of Spacing in Template Strings (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/template-curly-spacing" rel="nofollow">template-curly-spacing</a>) [1%]</li>
<li>Template strings are only allowed when necessary, i.e. template string features are being used (eslint got stricter: <a href="https://github.com/eslint/eslint/issues/5147" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/eslint/eslint/issues/5147/hovercard">eslint/eslint#5147</a>) [1%]</li>
<li>Better dead code detection after conditional statements (eslint got stricter) [1%]</li>
<li>Enforce spaces around <code>*</code> in <code>yield * something</code> (<a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/335" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/335/hovercard">#335</a>) (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/yield-star-spacing" rel="nofollow">yield-star-spacing</a>) [0%]</li>
<li>Disallow labels on loops/switch statements too (made rule stricter) (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/no-labels.html" rel="nofollow">no-labels</a>) [0%]</li>
<li>Disallow unnecessary constructor (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/no-useless-constructor" rel="nofollow">no-useless-constructor</a>) [0%]</li>
<li>Disallow empty destructuring patterns (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/no-empty-pattern" rel="nofollow">no-empty-pattern</a>) [0%]</li>
<li>Disallow Symbol Constructor (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/no-new-symbol" rel="nofollow">no-new-symbol</a>) [0%]</li>
<li>Disallow Self Assignment (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/no-self-assign" rel="nofollow">no-self-assign</a>) [0%]</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Removed Rules</h3><a id="user-content-removed-rules-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Removed Rules" href="#removed-rules-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>parseInt()</code> radix rule because ES5 fixes this issue (<a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/384" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/384/hovercard">#384</a>) (<a href="https://eslint.org/docs/2.0.0/rules/radix.html" rel="nofollow">radix</a>) [0%]</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Expose eslint configuration via command line options and <code>package.json</code></h3><a id="user-content-expose-eslint-configuration-via-command-line-options-and-packagejson" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Expose eslint configuration via command line options and package.json" href="#expose-eslint-configuration-via-command-line-options-and-packagejson"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For power users, it might be easier to use one of these new hooks instead of forking
<code>standard</code>, though that's still encouraged, too!</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Set eslint "plugins" (<a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/386" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/386/hovercard">#386</a>)</li>
<li>Set eslint "rules" (<a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/367" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/367/hovercard">#367</a>)</li>
<li>Set eslint "env" (<a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/issues/371" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/standard/standard/issues/371/hovercard">#371</a>)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">To set custom ESLint plugins, rules, or envs, use the command line <code>--plugin</code>, <code>--rules</code>, and <code>--env</code> flags.</p>
<p dir="auto">In <code>package.json</code>, use the "standard" property:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;standard&quot;: {
    &quot;plugins&quot;: [ &quot;my-plugin&quot; ]
  }
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"standard"</span>: {
    <span class="pl-ent">"plugins"</span>: [ <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>my-plugin<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ]
  }
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Upgrade to ESLint v2</h3><a id="user-content-upgrade-to-eslint-v2" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Upgrade to ESLint v2" href="#upgrade-to-eslint-v2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>There may be slight behavior changes to existing rules. When possible, we've noted these in the "New Rules" and "Removed Rules" section.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Improve test suite</h3><a id="user-content-improve-test-suite" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Improve test suite" href="#improve-test-suite"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v4.5.4...v5.0.0">5.0.0</a> - 2015-08-03</h2><a id="user-content-500---2015-08-03" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5.0.0 - 2015-08-03" href="#500---2015-08-03"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/standard/standard/compare/v4.5.4...v5.0.0">view diff</a></p>
<p dir="auto">eslint v1.0.0 is released! eslint added some new rules that are nice, and lots of existing rules have subtle behavior changes designed to catch more errors.</p>
<p dir="auto">Let's talk about the next version of standard! We bumped the major version to v5.0.0 to pull in these improvements.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">New rules:</h4><a id="user-content-new-rules-10" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: New rules:" href="#new-rules-10"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>space before/after arrow functions (<a href="https://github.com/feross/eslint-config-standard/commit/cf31561306f102b0772de55cd410b20912e733ee">https://github.com/feross/eslint-config-standard/commit/cf31561306f102b0772de55cd410b20912e733ee</a>)</li>
<li>indent switch "case" sections (<a href="https://github.com/feross/eslint-config-standard/commit/c6b10f68aa31e323933b14e04b50d8c1075ef28c">https://github.com/feross/eslint-config-standard/commit/c6b10f68aa31e323933b14e04b50d8c1075ef28c</a>)</li>
<li>don't reassign class variable names (<a href="https://github.com/feross/eslint-config-standard/commit/96c727fdf917f213e23320cc9971a0e2e5bf2b7b">https://github.com/feross/eslint-config-standard/commit/96c727fdf917f213e23320cc9971a0e2e5bf2b7b</a>)</li>
<li>don't reassign const variables (<a href="https://github.com/feross/eslint-config-standard/commit/2dd1a09edcff6656731a394231e93850e55cc39d">https://github.com/feross/eslint-config-standard/commit/2dd1a09edcff6656731a394231e93850e55cc39d</a>)</li>
<li>don't use .call() or .apply() to invoke a function unless it's necessary (<a href="https://github.com/feross/eslint-config-standard/commit/6fba6e34d9281a716bf7ffc9fc5d804f6403f505">https://github.com/feross/eslint-config-standard/commit/6fba6e34d9281a716bf7ffc9fc5d804f6403f505</a>)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Changed rules:</h4><a id="user-content-changed-rules-12" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Changed rules:" href="#changed-rules-12"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>use <code>no-extra-parens</code> instead of the deprecated <code>no-wrap-func</code> rule (<a href="https://github.com/feross/eslint-config-standard/commit/fc8a076c156d949b0b6046281f2e5f5c91e7da62">https://github.com/feross/eslint-config-standard/commit/fc8a076c156d949b0b6046281f2e5f5c91e7da62</a>)</li>
<li><code>indent</code> got stricter and catches errors in object literal indentation. 12/131 repos in the test suite started failing after this rule was improved.</li>
</ul>
